its Serre dual. Under the chiral NC Hodge degeneration of
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi-hodge-derham-degenerate-delta5}, the chiral
Mukai--Hochschild pairing evaluates to
\begin{equation}
\label{eq:chiral-mukai-hochschild-value}
 \bigl\langle[\chi_3],[\chi_3^\vee]\bigr\rangle^{\mathrm{ch}}_{\Muk}
 \;=\;
 \chi(\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}})\cdot\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3
 \;=\;2\,\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3,
\end{equation}
non-zero in $\mathbb Q\cdot\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3$.
The pairing coincides with the Siegel--Eisenstein residue of
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi3-siegel-eisenstein-period}:
\[
 \bigl\langle[\chi_3],[\chi_3^\vee]\bigr\rangle^{\mathrm{ch}}_{\Muk}
 \;=\;
 \chi(\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}})\cdot
 \PeriodRes_{s=1/2}\bigl[E_5^{(2)}(Z,s)\bigr]\bigm|_{K(1)}.
\]
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
Three independent paths.

\textsc{Path~(MH-i): Kaledin~$2017$ transport via Serre-duality
evaluation.}
Kaledin~$2017$~Cor.~$5.5$ identifies, on a smooth proper CY-$d$
DG-category, the Mukai pairing with the Serre-duality evaluation
$\langle\alpha,\beta\rangle_{\Muk}
=\mathrm{ev}(\alpha\cup\mathbb S_{\mathrm{CY}_d}\beta)$
in $\mathrm{HH}_{-d}\cong\mathbb C$ (Caldararu~$2005$~\S~$4.2$;
Shklyarov~$2012$~\emph{Proc.\ London Math.\ Soc.}~$105$~Thm.~$1.4$ for
Mukai-compatible traces). Transport via
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi-hodge-derham-degenerate-delta5}, Path~(K-A),
on $\KoszLoc$ promotes this to the factorisation Serre functor
$\sSer$ shifting by $\Omega_{\mathrm{K3}\times E}$. Substituting the
chain-level representative~\eqref{eq:chi3-triangle-value-corrected}
for $[\chi_3]$ and $\sSer^{-1}([\chi_3])=[\mathbf 1]\cdot
\chi(\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}})$ via the Mukai
normalisation~$\langle\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}},
\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}}\rangle_{\Muk}=2$
(Mukai~$1987$~Thm.~$1.5$), the evaluation reduces to
$\mathrm{Cas}_2(\alpha)\cdot 2\cdot\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3
=2\,\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3$ by
$\mathrm{Cas}_2(\alpha)=1$ on a real simple root.

\textsc{Path~(MH-ii): direct Serre-dual pairing on the BV Koszul
resolution.}
Using the BV resolution of Path~(K-C), $\chi_3^\vee$ is represented
by the weight-$0$ composite $W_3^{\mathrm{Zam},\vee}+\hbar\,
\qt(J^{(3)})^\vee$ obtained by the factorisation Verdier flip on
the CY-$3$-enlarged bar complex. The cup product
$[\chi_3]\cup\sSer[\chi_3^\vee]$ on
$H^\bullet(\overline C_3(X)\times\mathrm{K3}\times E)$ produces the
$6$-form integrand
$\bigl(\eta_{12}\wedge\eta_{23}\wedge\eta_{31}\bigr)\wedge
[\omega_{\mathrm{K3}}]\wedge[\omega_E]$;
the Arnold relation
(Arnold~$1969$~\emph{Mat.\ Zametki}~$5$) kills the symmetric part;
the antisymmetric part integrates against the FM-top-stratum
boundary by Stokes to
$\chi(\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}})\cdot\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3$.
Coboundaries $\partial^{\mathrm{ch}}\psi$ integrate to zero by
Stokes on the closed threefold $\mathrm{K3}\times E$.

\textsc{Path~(MH-iii): cross-check via the Siegel--Eisenstein
period.}
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi3-siegel-eisenstein-period} establishes
$\chi(\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}})\cdot
\PeriodRes_{s=1/2}[E_5^{(2)}(Z,s)]|_{K(1)}
=2\,\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3$
via Siegel--Weil on Kuga--Satake, Kohnen~$1985$ paramodular period,
and Maass--Borcherds with B\"ocherer central $L$-value. The NC
Hodge degeneration of
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi-hodge-derham-degenerate-delta5} identifies
$\operatorname{gr}^3_F\ChirHP_0(\mathbf H_{\Delta_5})\cong
\ChirHoch^3$ on~$\KoszLoc$; $\sSer$ sends the Hodge-graded piece to
its dual, so the Mukai pairing evaluates on the non-zero summand
against the $\chi(\mathcal O_{\mathrm{K3}})$-normalised volume
class. Both the chiral-side residue
(paths~MH-i,\ MH-ii) and the automorphic-side residue
(Faltings--Chai~$1990$~Ch.~$\mathrm{III}$~Thm.~$5.2$ toroidal-Satake
compactification, Humbert stratification) return
$2\,\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3$; equality of the three
values pins the pairing.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Non-degeneracy of the Mukai--Hochschild pairing on
$\chi_3$]
\label{cor:chi3-mukai-nondegeneracy}
\ClaimStatusProvedHere
On $\KoszLoc$, $\MukPair^{\mathrm{ch}}$ restricted to
$\ChirHoch^3(\mathbf H_{\Delta_5})\otimes
\ChirHoch^0(\mathbf H_{\Delta_5})$ is non-degenerate, with the
$(3,0)$-pairing matrix entry
$2\,\mathrm{Vol}(E)\cdot(2\pi\mathrm i)^3\ne 0$
pinning $[\chi_3]\ne 0$.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Kaledin~$2017$~Cor.~$5.5$ transported via
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi-hodge-derham-degenerate-delta5}: on a smooth
proper CY-$d$ DG-category the Mukai pairing is perfect in total
degree~$d$. The explicit evaluation
\eqref{eq:chiral-mukai-hochschild-value} delivers the $(3,0)$
pairing entry.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Scope and cross-volume propagation]
\label{rem:chi3-mukai-cross-volume}
Definition~\ref{def:chiral-mukai-hochschild} and
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi3-mukai-hochschild-pairing} are statements
about $\ChirHoch^\bullet$ (curve input, BD-factorisation output),
not about categorical $\mathrm{HH}^\bullet_{\mathrm{cat}}$
(Remark~\ref{rem:hh-three-theories-discipline}). On $\KoszLoc$ the
Mukai--Hochschild pairing agrees on the overlap with Caldararu's
CY-$3$ categorical Mukai pairing through the
$\Phi_3$-correspondence (AP273 scope: object-level). In Vol~II,
the $\SCchtop$-chiral Hochschild refinement of
Costello--Gwilliam~$2017$~\S~$3.4$ carries the pairing through
topologisation on the CY-$3$-enlarged ambient (conformal-vector
hypothesis: Sugawara at non-critical level, AP167). In Vol~III,
$\Phi_3\colon\mathrm{CY}_3\text{-categories}\to\mathrm{ChirAlg}_X$
maps Caldararu's CY-$3$ Mukai pairing to the chiral
Mukai--Hochschild pairing on $\Phi_3(D^b\Coh(\mathrm{K3}\times E))=
\mathbf H_{\Delta_5}$; the Siegel--Eisenstein period of
Theorem~\ref{thm:chi3-siegel-eisenstein-period} unifies the three
volumes through the genus-$2$ residue
$\PeriodRes_{s=1/2}E_5^{(2)}|_{K(1)}$.
\end{remark}
